## Get Allegro pickup drop off points

Get a list of Allegro pickup drop off points. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-przesylkami-przez-wysylam-z-allegro-LRVjK7K21sY#jak-pobrac-liste-punktow-allegro)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-manage-parcels-via-ship-with-allegro-ZM9YAyGKWTV#how-to-retrieve-list-of-allegro-pickup-drop-off-points).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-applicationbearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

Array of strings (AllegroCarrier)

Items Enum: "UPS" "ALLEGRO_ONE_KURIER" "DPD"

Example: carriers=ALLEGRO_ONE_KURIER

List of carrier ids to filter the drop off/pick up points to only the ones where any of the listed carriers operate. In case of an empty list, all points are returned.

| carriers |
| --- |

##### header Parameters

string <,:: GMT>

Example: Sat, 01 Dec 2018 10:00:00 GMT

Date of last data modification. If data has been modified after specified date, full set of data is returned. If header is not specified, full set of data is returned. Date has to be provided in HTTP-date format. Information about date (the same HTTP-date format) of last modified data is available in response -`Last-Modified`.

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| If-Modified-Since |
| --- |
| Accept-Language |

### Responses

200

Returns a list of Allegro pickup drop off points

304

Data has not been modified after the date provided in If-Modified-Since header.

400

Bad request. Invalid query parameters.

401

Authentication failed, e.g. token is expired

get/order/carriers/ALLEGRO/points

# Payments

## Payment operations history

Use this endpoint to get the list of the seller payment operations. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-sprawdzic-oplaty-nn9DOL5PASX#historia-operacji-platniczych)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-check-the-fees-3An6Wame3Um#payment-operations).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

string

Default: "AVAILABLE"

Enum: "AVAILABLE" "WAITING"

Type of the wallet: * AVAILABLE - operations available for payout. * WAITING - operations temporarily suspended for payout.

string

Enum: "PAYU" "P24" "AF" "AF_P24" "AF_PAYU"

Payment operator: * PAYU - operations processed by PAYU operator. * P24 - operations processed by PRZELEWY24 operator. * AF - operations processed by Allegro Finance operator. * AF_P24 - operations processed by Allegro Finance with PRZELEWY24. * AF_PAYU - operations processed by Allegro Finance with PAYU.

string 

The payment ID.

string

Login of the participant. In case of REFUND_INCREASE operation this is the login of the seller, in other cases, of the buyer.

string 

Example: occurredAt.gte=2019-05-08T09:45:20.818Z

The minimum date and time of operation occurrence in ISO 8601 format.

string 

Example: occurredAt.lte=2019-05-08T09:45:20.818Z

The maximum date and time of operation occurrence in ISO 8601 format.

Array of strings

Items Enum: "INCOME" "OUTCOME" "REFUND" "BLOCKADES"

Group of operation types: * INCOME - CONTRIBUTION, SURCHARGE, CORRECTION, DEDUCTION_INCREASE, LOAN_DEDUCTION_INCREASE, COMPENSATION, COMPENSATION_COD_INCREASE, TOP_UP. * OUTCOME - PAYOUT, PAYOUT_CANCEL, DEDUCTION_CHARGE, LOAN_DEDUCTION_CHARGE, COMPENSATION_COD_CHARGE. * REFUND - REFUND_CHARGE, REFUND_CANCEL, REFUND_INCREASE, CORRECTION, PROVIDER_REFUND_TRANSFER_CHARGE, PROVIDER_REFUND_TRANSFER_INCREASE. * BLOCKADES - BLOCKADE, BLOCKADE_RELEASE.

string

Enum: "allegro-pl" "allegro-cz"

Example: marketplaceId=allegro-pl

The marketplace ID where operation was made. When the parameter is omitted, searches for operations with all marketplaces. Note, that there are operations not assigned to any marketplace.

string

Example: currency=PLN

Currency of the operations.

integer [ 1 .. 50 ]

Default: 50

Number of returned operations.

integer [ 0 .. 10000 ]

Default: 0

Index of the first returned payment operation from all search results.

| wallet.type |
| --- |
| wallet.paymentOperator |
| payment.id |
| participant.login |
| occurredAt.gte |
| occurredAt.lte |
| group |
| marketplaceId |
| currency |
| limit |
| offset |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

200

The payment operations history for given search criteria returned successfully.

401

Unauthorized

422

Returned when any of the given search parameters have an invalid value or when the search result reached the limit of found operations - 10000.

get/payments/payment-operations

### Response samples

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

## Initiate a refund of a payment

Use this endpoint to initiate a refund of a payment. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-obslugiwac-zamowienia-GRaj0qyvwtR#jak-wykonac-zwrot-platnosci)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/process-orders-PgPMlWDr8Cv#how-to-refund-a-payment).

Array of objects (RefundLineItem)

Array of objects (RefundLineItemDeposit)

List of refundable deposits for the order's line items.

object

object

object

## Get the messages and state claim changes within a post purchase issue

##### path Parameters

required

string

##### query Parameters

integer [ 1 .. 100 ]

Default: 10

integer >= 0

Default: 0

Index of first returned message within issue.

| --- |
| offset |

## Add a message to an issue

Use this resource to post a message in certain issue. At least one of fields: 'text', 'attachment' has to be present. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-dyskusjami-E7Zj6gK7ysE#nowa-wiadomosc-w-dyskusji-lub-reklamacji)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-manage-discussions-VL6Yr40e5t5#new-message-in-dispute-or-claim).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

issueId

required

string 

Dispute or claim identifier.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.beta.v1+json

Message request

text

required

string <= 20000 characters

Array of objects (PostPurchaseIssueAttachmentId)

type

required

string

Enum: "REGULAR" "END_REQUEST" "RETURN_REQUIRED_SELLER_LABEL" "RETURN_REQUIRED_CUSTOM" "RETURN_NOT_REQUIRED"

Type of message,`END_REQUEST` is only allowed for disputes while return-related types are only allowed for claims.

| attachments |
| --- |

### Responses

201

Created

400

Bad Request

401

Unauthorized

403

Forbidden

404

Not Found

409

Dispute is in a state that forbids adding new messages

422

Unprocessable Entity

post/sale/issues/{issueId}/message

## Change status of a claim

Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-dyskusjami-E7Zj6gK7ysE#zmien-status-reklamacji)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-manage-discussions-VL6Yr40e5t5#change-claim-status).

string

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

required

string

Enum: "ACCEPTED_REPAIR" "ACCEPTED_REFUND" "ACCEPTED_EXCHANGE" "ACCEPTED_PARTIAL_REFUND" "REJECTED_ADDITIONAL_REQUIREMENTS_NOT_COMPLETED" "REJECTED_PRODUCT_NOT_RETURNED" "REJECTED_PRODUCT_DAMAGED_BY_USER" "REJECTED_PRODUCT_CONFORMS_TO_CONTRACT" "REJECTED_MINOR_DEFECT" "REJECTED_OTHER"

message

required

string

object (Price)

The price data.

| --- |

## Upload an attachment

Upload a post purchase issue message attachment. This operation should be used after creating an attachment declaration with POST /sale/issues/attachments Important! You can find the URL address to upload the file to our server in the Location response header of POST /sale/issues/attachments. The URL is unique and one-time. As its format may change in time, you should always use the address from the header. Do not compose the address on your own. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-dyskusjami-E7Zj6gK7ysE#dodanie-zalacznika)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-manage-discussions-VL6Yr40e5t5#adding-an-attachment).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

attachmentId

required

string 

Attachment identifier.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: image/pngimage/gifimage/bmpimage/tiffimage/jpegapplication/pdfimage/png

string 

File in a binary format

### Responses

200

File uploaded correctly

400

Syntactically incorrect request

401

Invalid or missing bearer token

413

File is too big

415

Unsupported media type

422

Unprocessable Entity

put/sale/issues/attachments/{attachmentId}

### Response samples

- 200

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.beta.v1+json

Copy

`{"id": "0c3c607d-d1de-4c6e-8db7-48c5b88a795d"}`

# Customer returns

## [BETA] Get customer returns by provided query parameters

Use this resource to get all customer returns filtered by query parameters. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-obslugiwac-zamowienia-GRaj0qyvwtR#jak-pobrac-liste-zwrotow)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/process-orders-PgPMlWDr8Cv#how-to-retrieve-customer-returns-list). This resource is limited to 25 requests per second for a single user and 50 requests per second for clientId.

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

string

One or more customer return id's.

string

One or more order id's.

string

One or more buyer emails.

string

One or more buyer logins.

string

One or more returned item offer id's.

string

One or more item names.

string

One or more waybill id's.

string

Waybill ids as generated by carriers physically transporting the parcel. Will be null if there's only one carrier involved in a parcel shipment.

string

One or more carrier id's.

string

Carrier id of a carrier physically transporting the parcel. Will be null if there's only one carrier involved in a parcel shipment.

string

One or more phone numbers.

string

One or more reference numbers.

string

The ID of the last seen customer return. Customer returns created after the given customer return will be returned.

string

Date of the return in ISO 8601 format to search by greater or equal.

string

Date of the return in ISO 8601 format to search by lower or equal.

string

The marketplace ID where operation was made. When the parameter is omitted, searches for operations with all marketplaces.

string

Current return timeline statuses. The allowed values are:

- WAREHOUSE_VERIFICATION.
- WAREHOUSE_DELIVERED
- COMMISSION_REFUNDED
- COMMISSION_REFUND_CLAIMED
- REJECTED
- FINISHED_APT
- FINISHED
- DELIVERED
- IN_TRANSIT
- DISPATCHED
- CREATED

integer [ 1 .. 1000 ]

Default: 100

Limit of customer returns per page.

integer >= 0

Default: 0

The offset of elements in the response.

| customerReturnId |
| --- |
| orderId |
| buyer.email |
| buyer.login |
| items.offerId |
| items.name |
| parcels.waybill |
| parcels.transportingWaybill |
| parcels.carrierId |
| parcels.transportingCarrierId |
| parcels.sender.phoneNumber |
| referenceNumber |
| from |
| createdAt.gte |
| createdAt.lte |
| marketplaceId |
| status |
| limit |
| offset |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

200

Successfully retrieved customer returns.

400

Bad request.

401

Unauthorized

403

Forbidden

406

Not Acceptable

get/order/customer-returns

### Response samples

- 406
- 403
- 401
- 400
- 200

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.beta.v1+json

422

## Create a warranty attachment metadata

You can attach PDF files to warranties. Uploading attachments flow:

1. Create (or update) warranty with attachment (POST /after-sales-service-conditions/warranties).
2. Use the upload URL to submit the PDF file (PUT /after-sales-service-conditions/attachments/{attachmentId}),
3. Create an attachment object to receive an upload URL (POST /after-sales-service-conditions/attachments),

Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-ofertami-7GzB2L37ase#jak-dodac-zalacznik-do-informacji-o-gwarancjach)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-process-list-of-offers-m09BKA5v8H3#how-to-add-attachment-to-warranty-information).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

After sale services attachment

string

| name |
| --- |

400

## Upload an warranty attachment

Upload an after sale services attachment. This operation should be used after creating an offer attachment with POST /sale/offer-attachments Important! You can find the URL address to upload the file to our server in the Location response header of POST /after-sales-service-conditions/attachments. The URL is unique and one-time. As its format may change in time, you should always use the address from the header. Do not compose the address on your own. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-ofertami-7GzB2L37ase#jak-dodac-zalacznik-do-informacji-o-gwarancjach)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-process-list-of-offers-m09BKA5v8H3#how-to-add-attachment-to-warranty-information).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

attachmentId

required

string

The ID of the attachment.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/pdf

string 

File in a binary format

### Responses

200

File uploaded correctly.

400

Syntactically incorrect request.

401

Invalid or missing bearer token.

403

Forbidden

404

Not found.

413

Payload too large.

422

Invalid file content.

## Get the user's delivery settings

Use this resource to get the delivery settings declared by the seller. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-kontem-danymi-uzytkownika-ZM9YAKgPgi2#jak-pobrac-ustawienia-dostawy)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/account-and-user-data-management-jn9vBjqjnsw#how-to-get-delivery-settings).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

string

Example: marketplace.id=allegro-pl

Marketplace for which delivery settings will be returned. By default (if the marketplace parameter is not set) the marketplace on which the seller has registered is used. However, we recommend that the marketplace.id query parameter should always be explicitly set.

| marketplace.id |
| --- |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

## Modify the user's delivery settings

Use this resource to modify the delivery settings declared by the seller. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-kontem-danymi-uzytkownika-ZM9YAKgPgi2#jak-edytowac-ustawienia-dostawy)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/account-and-user-data-management-jn9vBjqjnsw#how-to-edit-delivery-settings).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Delivery settings set

object

The marketplace for which delivery settings will be modified. By default (if the marketplace parameter is not set) the marketplace on which the seller has registered is used. However, we recommend that the marketplace parameter should always be explicitly set.

object

A minimum total order amount required to qualify for free domestic delivery (for example for allegro-cz marketplace, only Czechia is treated as domestic). If you do not want to set free domestic delivery threshold, do not set this value.

object

A minimum total order amount required to qualify for free foreign delivery (for example for allegro-cz marketplace, all delivery countries other than Czechia are treated as foreign). If you do not want to set free foreign delivery threshold, do not set this value.

joinPolicy

required

object

Policy of calculating delivery costs.

customCost

required

object

Policy of custom delivery cost.

| marketplace |
| --- |
| freeDelivery |
| abroadFreeDelivery |

### Responses

200

OK

401

Authentication required.

403

Forbidden - not allowed to access user data.

422

Unprocessable Entity - wrong amount, wrong currency, wrong join policy strategy, unsupported marketplace, attempt to modify marketplace allegro-business-* - modifying the settings for such a marketplace should be done by modifying the allegro-* marketplace.

required

string [ 1 .. 100 ] characters

# Points of service

## Create a point of service

Use this resource to create a point of service. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/news/punkty-odbioru-osobistego-8dmlj8qk7ik)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/news/points-of-service-Rdoz09ZE7sW).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Point of service

string

UUID. When creating a point of service (Post) the field is ignored. It is required when updating (Put) a point of service.

string <= 80 characters

ID from external client system.

name

required

string <= 80 characters

object (Seller)

type

required

string

Indicates point type. The only valid value so far is PICKUP_POINT.

address

required

object (Address)

string <= 16 characters

string <= 64 characters

Array of objects (PosLocation)

IDs for a location. When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

openHours

required

Array of objects (OpenHour)

Possible empty list of opening hours.

string

Delivery time / Time period for receipt. Date format ISO 8601 e.g. 'PT24H'

Array of objects (Payment)

An empty list of payment types is available.

confirmationType

required

string

Confirmation method: AWAIT_CONTACT - We will inform you about the time of receipt, CALL_US - Please make an appointment, CONTACT_NOT_REQUIRED - Contact is not required.

status

required

string

Point of service status: ACTIVE - active, TEMPORARILY_CLOSED - temporarily closed, CLOSED_DOWN - closed down, DELETED - deleted.

string

Creation date. Date format (ISO 8601) - yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSSZ When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

string

Modification date. Date format (ISO 8601) - yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSSZ When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

| id |
| --- |
| externalId |
| seller |
| phoneNumber |
| email |
| locations |
| serviceTime |
| payments |
| createdAt |
| updatedAt |

Forbidden

User identifier.

string

Example: countryCode=PL

Country code identifier in ISO format. In case of incorrect or unsupported country code, empty list is returned. If missing, list of all defined points is returned. If present, correct and supported, list of all points with given country code for the user is returned.

## Modify a point of service

Use this resource to modify a point of service. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/news/punkty-odbioru-osobistego-8dmlj8qk7ik)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/news/points-of-service-Rdoz09ZE7sW).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

id

required

string

Point of service ID. Must match values with 'id' property from the body.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: pl-PL

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Point of service

string

UUID. When creating a point of service (Post) the field is ignored. It is required when updating (Put) a point of service.

string <= 80 characters

ID from external client system.

name

required

string <= 80 characters

object (Seller)

type

required

string

Indicates point type. The only valid value so far is PICKUP_POINT.

address

required

object (Address)

string <= 16 characters

string <= 64 characters

Array of objects (PosLocation)

IDs for a location. When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

openHours

required

Array of objects (OpenHour)

Possible empty list of opening hours.

string

Delivery time / Time period for receipt. Date format ISO 8601 e.g. 'PT24H'

Array of objects (Payment)

An empty list of payment types is available.

confirmationType

required

string

Confirmation method: AWAIT_CONTACT - We will inform you about the time of receipt, CALL_US - Please make an appointment, CONTACT_NOT_REQUIRED - Contact is not required.

status

required

string

Point of service status: ACTIVE - active, TEMPORARILY_CLOSED - temporarily closed, CLOSED_DOWN - closed down, DELETED - deleted.

string

Creation date. Date format (ISO 8601) - yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSSZ When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

string

Modification date. Date format (ISO 8601) - yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss.SSSZ When creating (Post) or updating (Put) a point of service the field is ignored.

| --- |

| seller |
| phoneNumber |
| email |

| payments |

| updatedAt |

# Advance Ship Notices

## Get list of Advance Ship Notices

Use this resource to get a list of Advance Ship Notices. The list is ordered by createdAt property. Default offset is 0, default limit is 50. A list can be filtered by statuses. Multiple status query parameters are allowed. In such cases, filters are joined with OR logical operator. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#jak-przegladac-utworzone-awizo)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#how-to-get-created-advance-ship-notices).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

integer >= 0

Default: 0

The offset of elements in the response.

integer [ 1 .. 200 ]

Default: 50

Maximum number of elements in response.

Array of strings (AdvanceShipNoticeStatus)

Items Enum: "DRAFT" "IN_TRANSIT" "UNPACKING" "COMPLETED" "CANCELLED"

Example: status=DRAFT

A status of the Advance Ship Notices in the response.

| offset |
| --- |
| limit |
| status |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

200

Returns list of Advance Ship Notices that belong to a seller.

401

Unauthorized

403

Forbidden

422

Invalid request parameters.

get/fulfillment/advance-ship-notices

### Response samples

- 422
- 200

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Copy

Expand all Collapse all

[https://api.allegro.pl/fulfillment/678453232](https://api.allegro.pl/fulfillment/678453232)

`{"advanceShipNotices": [{"id": "71529ad2-2265-4e15-b76b-c17025d848f7","displayNumber": "A-210310-0000002","status": "DRAFT","createdAt": "2020-08-26T12:50:04Z","updatedAt": "2020-08-26T12:52:04Z","items": [{"product": {"id": "a1520fab-7801-4832-9ccd-fb068c707a74"},"quantity": 1}],"handlingUnit": {"unitType": "BOX","amount": 1,"labelsType": "ONE_FULFILMENT"},"labels": {"fileUrl": ""},"shipping": {"method": "COURIER_BY_SELLER"},"submittedAt": "2020-08-26T12:52:04Z"}],"count": 1,"totalCount": 1}`

## Create an Advance Ship Notice

Use this resource to create an Advance Ship Notice. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#utworz-draft-awizo)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#create-a-draft-of-the-advance-ship-notice).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

items

required

Array of objects (ProductItem)

A list of product items.

object (HandlingUnit)

Represents information about handling unit.

object (Shipping)

Represents information about package shipment. Constraints:

- for method THIRD_PARTY_DELIVERY: thirdParty, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method COURIER_BY_SELLER: courier, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method OWN_TRANSPORT: truckLicencePlate, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.

number (DeclaredAsnVolume)

Total volume of all items declared by the merchant for delivery to the warehouse as part of the advance shipment notice, in cubic centimeters.

| handlingUnit |
| --- |
| shipping |
| declaredVolumeInCc |

### Responses

201

Advance Ship Notice created.

400

Invalid request body.

401

Unauthorized

403

Forbidden

422

Advance Ship Notice cannot be created due to improper input data.

post/fulfillment/advance-ship-notices

### Request samples

- Payload

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Copy

Expand all Collapse all

- 422
- 400
- 201

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Copy

`{"id": "71529ad2-2265-4e15-b76b-c17025d848f7","displayNumber": "A-210310-0000002","status": "DRAFT","createdAt": "2020-08-26T12:50:04Z","updatedAt": "2020-08-26T12:50:04Z","items": [{"product": {"id": "a1520fab-7801-4832-9ccd-fb068c707a74"},"quantity": 1}],"handlingUnit": {"unitType": "BOX","amount": 1,"labelsType": "ONE_FULFILMENT"},"labels": {"fileUrl": ""},"shipping": {"method": "COURIER_BY_SELLER"},"volumeInCc": 1500}`

## Update Advance Ship Notice

Use this resource to update an Advance Ship Notice. Any content property update will clear labels property. Use Create labels command to create new labels for provided content. If a client wants to update read-only property, an error is returned (only in cases when sent value will be different than actual on the server). Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#uzupelnij-dane-o-awizo)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#complete-the-data-of-advance-ship-notice).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

id

required

string 

Example: 84529ad2-2265-4e15-b76b-c17025d848f6

An identifier of Advance Ship Notice.

##### header Parameters

if-match

required

string

Example: 123456

A current version of Advance Ship Notice (e.g. from etag header obtained via get).

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

items

required

Array of objects (ProductItem)

A list of product items.

object (HandlingUnit)

Represents information about handling unit.

object (Shipping)

Represents information about package shipment. Constraints:

- for method THIRD_PARTY_DELIVERY: thirdParty, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method COURIER_BY_SELLER: courier, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method OWN_TRANSPORT: truckLicencePlate, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.

number (DeclaredAsnVolume)

Total volume of all items declared by the merchant for delivery to the warehouse as part of the advance shipment notice, in cubic centimeters.

| handlingUnit |
| --- |
| shipping |
| declaredVolumeInCc |

### Responses

200

Advance Ship Notice updated

400

If-match header missing

401

Unauthorized

403

Forbidden

412

Concurrent modification of ASN

422

ASN is invalid or attempting to update read-only property

## Submit the Advance Ship Notice

Use this resource to submit the Advance Ship Notice. After this operation, updates of the Advance Ship Notice are limited to selected properties only. See [PUT /fulfillment/advance-ship-notices/{id}/submitted](https://developer.allegro.pl/documentation#operation/updateSubmittedAdvanceShipNotice). Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#zakoncz-edycje-i-wyslij-awizo)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#finish-editing-and-submit-the-advance-ship-notice).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

command-id

required

string 

Default: "725432a9-ae9e-43de-b8c5-7430606a81a4"

The identifier of the command.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

string 

The identifier of command.

input

required

object (SubmitCommandInput)

Represents input of the Advance Ship Notice submit command.

object (SubmitCommandOutput)

Represents output of the Advance Ship Notice submit command.

| id |
| --- |
| output |

### Responses

201

Returns command output with status and possible errors. The command could fail with following error codes:

- COMMAND_FAILED - Any other error.
- INVALID_ASN_STATE - Such command cannot be run on current ASN state e.g. ASN has no shipping information.
- COMMAND_FORBIDDEN - Requester has no access to run commands on given ASN.
- ASN_NOT_FOUND - Cannot find ASN with id given in command input.

401

Unauthorized

422

Invalid request parameters.

put/fulfillment/submit-commands/{command-id}

### Request samples

- Payload

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Copy

Expand all Collapse all

`{"id": "71529ad2-2265-4e15-b76b-c17025d848f7","input": {"advanceShipNoticeId": "123a08d7-ab9b-460d-b9cb-d6ed64b3a018"},"output": {"status": "RUNNING"}}`

### Response samples

- 422
- 201

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Example

Expand all Collapse all

## Update submitted Advance Ship Notice

Use this resource to update already submitted Advance Ship Notice. Update is allowed only when Advance Ship Notice is in "IN_TRANSIT" status. Handling unit's amount property update clears labels property. Use Create labels command to create new labels for provided content. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#edytuj-zakonczone-awizo)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#edit-advance-ship-notice).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

id

required

string 

Example: 84529ad2-2265-4e15-b76b-c17025d848f6

An identifier of Advance Ship Notice.

##### header Parameters

if-match

required

string

Example: 123456

A current version of Advance Ship Notice (e.g. from etag header obtained via get).

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Array of objects (ProductItem)

A list of product items.

object (HandlingUnit)

Represents information about handling unit.

object (Shipping)

Represents information about package shipment. Constraints:

- for method THIRD_PARTY_DELIVERY: thirdParty, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method COURIER_BY_SELLER: courier, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.
- for method OWN_TRANSPORT: truckLicencePlate, estimatedTimeOfArrival and countryCode are required.

number (DeclaredAsnVolume)

Total volume of all items declared by the merchant for delivery to the warehouse as part of the advance shipment notice, in cubic centimeters.

## Check current state and details of Advance Ship Notice receiving

Use this resource to check the state of Advance Ship Notice receiving in Fulfillment Center in real time. The response contains a receiving progress and information about particular items - their quantities and conditions. While the Advance Ship Notice is in UNPACKING state, report is updated dynamically, which might result in different responses even at short time intervals. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#sprawdz-postep-odbioru-awizo-przez-magazyn)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#check-current-state-and-details-of-advance-ship-notice-receiving).

# Fulfillment Stock

## Get available stock

Use this resource to get a list of the products belonging to the seller, which are in Allegro Warehouse. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#jak-pobrac-aktualne-stany-magazynowe)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#get-available-stock).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

integer >= 0

Default: 0

The offset of elements in the response. Ignored for text/csv content type.

integer [ 1 .. 1000 ]

Default: 50

Maximum number of elements in response. Ignored for text/csv content type.

string >= 3 characters

Filtering search results by product name.

string

Default: "name"

Enum: "available" "-available" "unfulfillable" "-unfulfillable" "name" "-name" "lastFourteenDaysSalesAverage" "-lastFourteenDaysSalesAverage" "reserve" "-reserve" "lastThirtyDaysSalesSum" "-lastThirtyDaysSalesSum" "storageFee" "-storageFee"

Defines how elements are sorted in response. Minus sign can be added to imply descending sort order. Ignored for text/csv content type. Possible values for the "sort" parameter:

- -storageFee - sorting by storage fee (descending). The order by fee status is: CHARGED ordered by amountGross descending, then NOT_APPLICABLE.
- storageFee - sorting by storage fee (ascending). The order by fee status is: NOT_APPLICABLE, then CHARGED ordered by amountGross ascending.
- -lastThirtyDaysSalesSum - sorting by product last month sum sales (descending)
- lastThirtyDaysSalesSum - sorting by product last month sum sales (ascending)
- -reserve - sorting by reserve.outOfStockIn field (descending)
- reserve - sorting by reserve.outOfStockIn field (ascending)
- -lastFourteenDaysSalesAverage - sorting by product last fourteen days average sales (descending)
- lastFourteenDaysSalesAverage - sorting by product last fourteen days average sales (ascending)
- name - sorting by product’s name (ascending)
- -name - sorting by product’s name (descending)
- unfulfillable - sorting by quantity of unfulfillable products (ascending)
- -unfulfillable - sorting by quantity of unfulfillable products (descending)
- available - sorting by quantity of available products (ascending)
- -available - sorting by quantity of available products (descending)

string 

Filtering search results by fulfillment product identifier. Ignored for text/csv content type.

Array of strings

Items Enum: "SUFFICIENT" "UNAVAILABLE" "LOW"

Filtering search results by availability.

string

Value: "UNFULFILLABLE"

Filtering search results by status.

string

Enum: "SUBMITTED" "NOT_FOUND"

Filtering search results by ASN status. Following values are allowed: SUBMITTED - Advanced Ship Notice document has been submitted and it contains a particular product. Only the products that have ASN with products on it are returned. NOT_FOUND - Advanced Ship Notice that contains a particular product was not found. It has not been submitted, may be expired, or products have already been delivered to the warehouse. Only the products that don't have related ASN with products on it are returned.

integer

Filter by products with outOfStockIn greater than or equal.

integer

Filter by products with outOfStockIn less than or equal.

| offset |
| --- |
| limit |
| phrase |
| sort |
| productId |
| productAvailability |
| productStatus |
| asnStatus |
| outOfStockInFrom |
| outOfStockInTo |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

# Fulfillment Removal

## Get current active removal preference

Use this resource to read your current removal preference. Removal preference is associated with system removal order at the moment of removal order is created. It means there can be not yet fulfilled removal orders associated with previously set removal preference. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#pobierz-aktualne-ustawienia-sposobu-usuniecia-towaru-z-magazynu)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#retrieve-current-settings-for-how-to-remove-goods-from-the-warehouse).

## Create new active Fulfillment Removal Preference

Use this resource to create new active removal preference. From the moment the preference is set, it becomes the active one, and all new system removal orders will be associated with this preference. Removal preference is associated with system removal order at the moment of removal order is created. It means there can be not yet fulfilled removal orders associated with previously set removal preference. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-0ADwgOLqWSw#utworz-lub-edytuj-ustawienia-sposobu-usuniecia-towaru-z-magazynu)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/one-fulfillment-by-allegro-4R9dXyMPlc9#create-or-edit-settings-for-how-to-remove-goods-from-the-warehouse).

##### Authorizations:

| --- |

Index of the first returned message from all results.

string 

Example: before=2020-11-13T12:45:20.818Z

Message creation date before filter parameter (exclusive) - cannot be used with offset.

string 

Example: after=2020-11-13T12:45:20.818Z

Message creation date after filter parameter (exclusive).

| limit |
| --- |
| offset |
| before |
| after |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

200

Thread message list returned successfully

401

User not authorized

403

User not allowed to list messages in selected thread

404

Thread not found

422

Incorrect limit, offset, after or before

get/messaging/threads/{threadId}/messages

## Write a new message in thread

Use this resource to write new message in existing thread. This resource is rate limited to 1 request per second for a user. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-zarzadzac-centrum-wiadomosci-XxWm2K890Fk#nowa-wiadomosc)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-manage-the-message-center-g05avyGlZUW#add-a-new-message).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### path Parameters

threadId

required

string

Identifier of thread to write message to.

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

##### Request Body schema: application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

text

required

string <= 2000 characters

Array of objects or null (MessageAttachmentId)

| attachments |
| --- |

### Responses

Message in thread successfully written

401

User not authorized

403

User not allowed to list messages in selected thread

404

Thread not found

422

Validation errors

# Billing

## Get a list of billing entries

The billing entries are sorted in a descending order (newest first) by date on which they occurred. Read more: [PL](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/jak-sprawdzic-oplaty-nn9DOL5PASX#historia-operacji-billingowych)/ [EN](https://developer.allegro.pl/tutorials/how-to-check-the-fees-3An6Wame3Um#billing-operations).

##### Authorizations:

bearer-token-for-user

##### query Parameters

string

Example: marketplaceId=allegro-pl

The marketplace ID where operation was made. By default the marketplace ID where the user is registered. Note: Business marketplace is not a separate user's billing and defaults back to the main marketplace for given country.

string 

Example: occurredAt.gte=2019-05-08T09:45:32.818Z

Date from which billing entries are filtered. If occurredAt.lte is also set, occurredAt.gte cannot be later.

string 

Example: occurredAt.lte=2019-05-08T09:45:32.818Z

Date to which billing entries are filtered. If occurredAt.gte is also set, occurredAt.lte cannot be earlier.

Array of strings

Example: type.id=LIS&type.id=SUC

List of billing types by which billing entries are filtered.

string

Example: offer.id=12345

Offer ID by which billing entries are filtered.

string 

Example: order.id=29738e61-7f6a-11e8-ac45-09db60ede9d6

Order UUID by which billing entries are filtered.

integer [ 1 .. 100 ]

Default: 100

Example: limit=10

Number of returned operations.

integer [ 0 .. 10000 ]

Default: 0

Example: offset=10

Index of the first returned payment operation from all search results.

| marketplaceId |
| --- |
| occurredAt.gte |
| occurredAt.lte |
| type.id |
| offer.id |
| order.id |
| limit |
| offset |

##### header Parameters

string 

Enum: "en-US" "pl-PL" "uk-UA" "sk-SK" "cs-CZ" "hu-HU"

Example: en-US

Expected language of messages.

| Accept-Language |
| --- |

### Responses

200

List of billing entries returned successfully.

401

Unauthorized

406

Not Acceptable

422

Unprocessable Entity

get/billing/billing-entries

### Response samples

- 422
- 406
- 401
- 200

Content type

application/vnd.allegro.public.v1+json

Copy

Expand all Collapse all

`{"billingEntries": [{"id": "09f0b4cc-7880-11e9-8f9e-2a86e4085a59","occurredAt": "2019-05-08T09:45:32.818Z","type": {"id": "LIS","name": "Listing fee"},"offer": {"id": "12345678","name": "offer name"},"value": {"amount": "100.00","currency": "PLN"},"tax": {"percentage": "0","annotation": "OUT_OF_SCOPE"},"balance": {"amount": "100.00","currency": "PLN"},"order": {"id": "09f0b4cc-7880-11e9-8f9e-2a86e4085a59"},"additionalInfo": [{"type": "additional_service","name": "Name of additional service","value": "55555555"}]}]}`
